none;</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;math <span class="html-attribute-name">xmlns</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML</span>"  <span class="html-attribute-name">alttext</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">{\displaystyle B}</span>"&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1002"></td><td class="line-content">  <span class="html-tag">&lt;semantics&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1003"></td><td class="line-content">    <span class="html-tag">&lt;mrow <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">MJX-TeXAtom-ORD</span>"&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1004"></td><td class="line-content">      <span class="html-tag">&lt;mstyle <span class="html-attribute-name">displaystyle</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">true</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">scriptlevel</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">0</span>"&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1005"></td><td class="line-content">        <span class="html-tag">&lt;mi&gt;</span>B<span class="html-tag">&lt;/mi&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1006"></td><td class="line-content">      <span class="html-tag">&lt;/mstyle&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1007"></td><td class="line-content">    <span class="html-tag">&lt;/mrow&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1008"></td><td class="line-content">    <span class="html-tag">&lt;annotation <span class="html-attribute-name">encoding</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">application/x-tex</span>"&gt;</span>{\displaystyle B}<span class="html-tag">&lt;/annotation&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1009"></td><td class="line-content">  <span class="html-tag">&lt;/semantics&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1010"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/math&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;img <span class="html-attribute-name">src</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-resource-link" target="_blank" href="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" rel="noreferrer noopener">https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mwe-math-fallback-image-inline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">aria-hidden</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">true</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">style</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">alt</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">B</span>"/&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span> is the number of bits per symbol). Another method is to simply prepend the Huffman tree, bit by bit, to the output stream. For example, assuming that the value of 0 represents a parent node and 1 a leaf node, whenever the latter is encountered the tree building routine simply reads the next 8 bits to determine the character value of that particular leaf. The process continues recursively until the last leaf node is reached; at that point, the Huffman tree will thus be faithfully reconstructed. The overhead using such a method ranges from roughly 2 to 320 bytes (assuming an 8-bit alphabet). Many other techniques are possible as well. In any case, since the compressed data can include unused "trailing bits" the decompressor must be able to determine when to stop producing output. This can be accomplished by either transmitting the length of the decompressed data along with the compression model or by defining a special code symbol to signify the end of input (the latter method can adversely affect code length optimality, however).</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1011"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1012"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h2&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Main_properties</span>"&gt;</span>Main properties<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" rel="noreferrer noopener">/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;section=10</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Edit section: Main properties</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h2&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1013"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>The probabilities used can be generic ones for the application domain that are based on average experience, or they can be the actual frequencies found in the text being compressed.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1014"></td><td class="line-content">This requires that a <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frequency_table" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Frequency_table</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Frequency table</span>"&gt;</span>frequency table<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> must be stored with the compressed text. See the Decompression section above for more information about the various techniques employed for this purpose.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1015"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1016"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h3&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Optimality</span>"&gt;</span>Optimality<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" rel="noreferrer noopener">/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;section=11</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Edit section: Optimality</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h3&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1017"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;dl&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;dd&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>See also <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arithmetic_coding#Huffman_coding" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Arithmetic_coding#Huffman_coding</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Arithmetic coding</span>"&gt;</span>Arithmetic coding#Huffman coding<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/dd&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/dl&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1018"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>Huffman's original algorithm is optimal for a symbol-by-symbol coding with a known input probability distribution, i.e., separately encoding unrelated symbols in such a data stream.  However, it is not optimal when the symbol-by-symbol restriction is dropped, or when the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Probability_mass_function" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Probability_mass_function</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Probability mass function</span>"&gt;</span>probability mass functions<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> are unknown.  Also, if symbols are not <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Independent_and_identically_distributed" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Independent_and_identically_distributed</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Independent and identically distributed</span>"&gt;</span>independent and identically distributed<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, a single code may be insufficient for optimality.  Other methods such as <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arithmetic_coding" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Arithmetic_coding</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Arithmetic coding</span>"&gt;</span>arithmetic coding<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> often have better compression capability.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1019"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>Although both aforementioned methods can combine an arbitrary number of symbols for more efficient coding and generally adapt to the actual input statistics, arithmetic coding does so without significantly increasing its computational or algorithmic complexities (though the simplest version is slower and more complex than Huffman coding).  Such flexibility is especially useful when input probabilities are not precisely known or vary significantly within the stream.  However, Huffman coding is usually faster and arithmetic coding was historically a subject of some concern over <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Patent" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Patent</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Patent</span>"&gt;</span>patent<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> issues.  Thus many technologies have historically avoided arithmetic coding in favor of Huffman and other prefix coding techniques.  As of mid-2010, the most commonly used techniques for this alternative to Huffman coding have passed into the public domain as the early patents have expired.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1020"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>For a set of symbols with a uniform probability distribution and a number of members which is a <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Power_of_two" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Power_of_two</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Power of two</span>"&gt;</span>power of two<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, Huffman coding is equivalent to simple binary <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Block_code" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Block_code</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Block code</span>"&gt;</span>block encoding<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, e.g., <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ASCII" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/ASCII</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">ASCII</span>"&gt;</span>ASCII<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> coding.  This reflects the fact that compression is not possible with such an input, no matter what the compression method, i.e., doing nothing to the data is the optimal thing to do.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1021"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>Huffman coding is optimal among all methods in any case where each input symbol is a known independent and identically distributed random variable having a probability that is <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dyadic_distribution" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Dyadic_distribution</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Dyadic distribution</span>"&gt;</span>dyadic<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>. Prefix codes, and thus Huffman coding in particular, tend to have inefficiency on small alphabets, where probabilities often fall between these optimal (dyadic) points. The worst case for Huffman coding can happen when the probability of the most likely symbol far exceeds 2<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup&gt;</span>1<span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> = 0.5, making the upper limit of inefficiency unbounded.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1022"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>There are two related approaches for getting around this particular inefficiency while still using Huffman coding.  Combining a fixed number of symbols together ("blocking") often increases (and never decreases) compression.  As the size of the block approaches infinity,  Huffman coding theoretically approaches the entropy limit, i.e., optimal compression.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-6</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Huffman_coding#cite_note-6" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-6</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;6&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span>  However, blocking arbitrarily large groups of symbols is impractical, as the complexity of a Huffman code is linear in the number of possibilities to be encoded, a number that is exponential in the size of a block.  This limits the amount of blocking that is done in practice.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1023"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>A practical alternative, in widespread use, is <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Run-length_encoding" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Run-length_encoding</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Run-length encoding</span>"&gt;</span>run-length encoding<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>.  This technique adds one step in advance of entropy coding, specifically counting (runs) of repeated symbols, which are then encoded.  For the simple case of <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bernoulli_process" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Bernoulli_process</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Bernoulli process</span>"&gt;</span>Bernoulli processes<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Golomb_coding" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Golomb_coding</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Golomb coding</span>"&gt;</span>Golomb coding<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> is optimal among prefix codes for coding run length, a fact proved via the techniques of Huffman coding.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-7</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Huffman_coding#cite_note-7" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-7</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;7&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span>  A similar approach is taken by fax machines using <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Modified_Huffman_coding" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Modified_Huffman_coding</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Modified Huffman coding</span>"&gt;</span>modified Huffman coding<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>.  However, run-length coding is not as adaptable to as many input types as other compression technologies.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1024"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1025"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h2&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Variations</span>"&gt;</span>Variations<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" rel="noreferrer noopener">/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;section=12</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Edit section: Variations</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h2&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1026"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>Many variations of Huffman coding exist,<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-8</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Huffman_coding#cite_note-8" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-8</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;8&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> some of which use a Huffman-like algorithm, and others of which find optimal prefix codes (while, for example, putting different restrictions on the output). Note that, in the latter case, the method need not be Huffman-like, and, indeed, need not even be <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polynomial_time" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Polynomial_time</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Polynomial time</span>"&gt;</span>polynomial time<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1027"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1028"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h3&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">n-ary_Huffman_coding</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>n<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>-ary Huffman coding<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" rel="noreferrer noopener">/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;section=13</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Edit section: n-ary Huffman coding</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h3&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1029"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>The <span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>n<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>-ary Huffman<span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span> algorithm uses the {0, 1,..., <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>n<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>  1} alphabet to encode message and build an <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>n<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>-ary tree. This approach was considered by Huffman in his original paper. The same algorithm applies as for binary (<span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>n<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> equals 2) codes, except that the <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>n<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> least probable symbols are taken together, instead of just the 2 least probable. Note that for <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>n<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> greater than 2, not all sets of source words can properly form an <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>n<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>-ary tree for Huffman coding. In these cases, additional 0-probability place holders must be added. This is because the tree must form an <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>n<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> to 1 contractor; for binary coding, this is a 2 to 1 contractor, and any sized set can form such a contractor.  If the number of source words is congruent to 1 modulo <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>n<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>-1, then the set of source words will form a proper Huffman tree.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1030"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1031"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h3&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Adaptive_Huffman_coding</span>"&gt;</span>Adaptive Huffman coding<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" rel="noreferrer noopener">/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;section=14</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Edit section: Adaptive Huffman coding</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h3&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1032"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>A variation called <span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adaptive_Huffman_coding" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Adaptive_Huffman_coding</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Adaptive Huffman coding</span>"&gt;</span>adaptive Huffman coding<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span> involves calculating the probabilities dynamically based on recent actual frequencies in the sequence of source symbols, and changing the coding tree structure to match the updated probability estimates. It is used rarely in practice, since the cost of updating the tree makes it slower than optimized <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arithmetic_coding#Adaptive_arithmetic_coding" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Arithmetic_coding#Adaptive_arithmetic_coding</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Arithmetic coding</span>"&gt;</span>adaptive arithmetic coding<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, which is more flexible and has better compression.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1033"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1034"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h3&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Huffman_template_algorithm</span>"&gt;</span>Huffman template algorithm<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" rel="noreferrer noopener">/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;section=15</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Edit section: Huffman template algorithm</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h3&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1035"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>Most often, the weights used in implementations of Huffman coding represent numeric probabilities, but the algorithm given above does not require this; it requires only that the weights form a <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Total_order" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Total_order</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Total order</span>"&gt;</span>totally ordered<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Monoid#Commutative_monoid" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Monoid#Commutative_monoid</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Monoid</span>"&gt;</span>commutative monoid<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, meaning a way to order weights and to add them. The <span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>Huffman template algorithm<span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span> enables one to use any kind of weights (costs, frequencies, pairs of weights, non-numerical weights) and one of many combining methods (not just addition). Such algorithms can solve other minimization problems, such as minimizing <span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mwe-math-element</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">style</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">display: none;</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;math <span class="html-attribute-name">xmlns</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML</span>"  <span class="html-attribute-name">alttext</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">{\displaystyle \max _{i}\left[w_{i}+\mathrm {length} \left(c_{i}\right)\right]}</span>"&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1036"></td><td class="line-content">  <span class="html-tag">&lt;semantics&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1037"></td><td class="line-content">    <span class="html-tag">&lt;mrow <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">MJX-TeXAtom-ORD</span>"&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1038"></td><td class="line-content">      <span class="html-tag">&lt;mstyle <span class="html-attribute-name">displaystyle</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">true</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">scriptlevel</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">0</span>"&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1039"></td><td class="line-content">        <span class="html-tag">&lt;munder&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1040"></td><td class="line-content">          <span class="html-tag">&lt;mo <span value="1134"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h3&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Huffman_coding_with_unequal_letter_costs</span>"&gt;</span>Huffman coding with unequal letter costs<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" rel="noreferrer noopener">/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;section=17</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Edit section: Huffman coding with unequal letter costs</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h3&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1135"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>In the standard Huffman coding problem, it is assumed that each symbol in the set that the code words are constructed from has an equal cost to transmit: a code word whose length is <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>N<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> digits will always have a cost of <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>N<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>, no matter how many of those digits are 0s, how many are 1s, etc. When working under this assumption, minimizing the total cost of the message and minimizing the total number of digits are the same thing.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1136"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>Huffman coding with unequal letter costs<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> is the generalization without this assumption: the letters of the encoding alphabet may have non-uniform lengths, due to characteristics of the transmission medium. An example is the encoding alphabet of <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Morse_code" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Morse_code</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Morse code</span>"&gt;</span>Morse code<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, where a 'dash' takes longer to send than a 'dot', and therefore the cost of a dash in transmission time is higher. The goal is still to minimize the weighted average codeword length, but it is no longer sufficient just to minimize the number of symbols used by the message. No algorithm is known to solve this in the same manner or with the same efficiency as conventional Huffman coding, though it has been solved by <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">rel</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">nofollow</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">external text</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="http://ieeexplore.ieee.org/xpl/articleDetails.jsp?arnumber=1057615&amp;newsearch=true&amp;queryText=Minimum-redundancy%20coding%20for%20the%20discrete%20noiseless%20channel" rel="noreferrer noopener">http://ieeexplore.ieee.org/xpl/articleDetails.jsp?arnumber=1057615&amp;amp;newsearch=true&amp;amp;queryText=Minimum-redundancy%20coding%20for%20the%20discrete%20noiseless%20channel</a>"&gt;</span>Karp<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> whose solution has been refined for the case of integer costs by <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">rel</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">nofollow</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">external text</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1137"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" problem,<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-9</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> which has some similarities to Huffman algorithm, but is not a variation of this algorithm. A later method, the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Garsia%E2%80%93Wachs_algorithm" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Garsia%E2%80%93Wachs_algorithm</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">GarsiaWachs algorithm</span>"&gt;</span>GarsiaWachs algorithm<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> of <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Adriano_Garsia" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Adriano_Garsia</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Adriano Garsia</span>"&gt;</span>Adriano Garsia<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> and <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michelle_L._Wachs" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Michelle_L._Wachs</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Michelle L. Wachs</span>"&gt;</span>Michelle L. Wachs<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> (1977), uses simpler logic to perform the same comparisons in the same total time bound. These optimal alphabetic binary trees are often used as <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" weights corresponding to the alphabetically ordered inputs are in numerical order, the Huffman code has the same lengths as the optimal alphabetic code, which can be found from calculating these lengths, rendering HuTucker coding unnecessary. The code resulting from numerically (re-)ordered input is sometimes called the <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>canonical Huffman code<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> and is often the code used in practice, due to ease of encoding/decoding. The technique for finding this code is sometimes called <span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>HuffmanShannonFano coding<span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span>, since it is optimal like Huffman coding, but alphabetic in weight probability, like <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shannon%E2%80%93Fano_coding" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Shannon%E2%80%93Fano_coding</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">ShannonFano coding</span>"&gt;</span>ShannonFano coding<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>. class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1309"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h2&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Applications</span>"&gt;</span>Applications<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" rel="noreferrer noopener">/w/index.php?title=Huffman_coding&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;section=20</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Edit section: Applications</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h2&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1310"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arithmetic_coding" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Arithmetic_coding</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Arithmetic coding</span>"&gt;</span>Arithmetic coding<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> and Huffman coding produce equivalent results &amp;#8212; achieving entropy &amp;#8212; when every symbol has a probability of the form 1/2<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>k<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span>.  In other circumstances, arithmetic coding can offer better compression than Huffman coding because &amp;#8212; intuitively &amp;#8212; its "code words" can have effectively non-integer bit lengths, whereas code words in prefix codes such as Huffman codes can only have an integer number of bits. Therefore, a code word of length <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>k<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> only optimally matches a symbol of probability 1/2<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>k<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> and other probabilities are not represented optimally; whereas the code word length in arithmetic coding can be made to exactly match the true probability of the symbol.  This difference is especially striking for small alphabet sizes.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1311"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>Prefix codes nevertheless remain in wide use because of their simplicity, high speed, and <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arithmetic_coding#History_and_patents" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Arithmetic_coding#History_and_patents</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Arithmetic coding</span>"&gt;</span>lack of patent coverage<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>.  They are often used as a "back-end" to other compression methods.  <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Deflate" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Deflate</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Deflate</span>"&gt;</span>Deflate<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> (<span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/PKZIP" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/PKZIP</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">PKZIP</span>"&gt;</span>PKZIP<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>'s algorithm) and multimedia <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Codec" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Codec</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Codec</span>"&gt;</span>codecs<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> such as <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/JPEG" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/JPEG</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">JPEG</span>"&gt;</span>JPEG<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> and <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MP3" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/MP3</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">MP3</span>"&gt;</span>MP3<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> have a front-end model and <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Quantization_(signal_processing)" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Quantization_(signal_processing)</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Quantization (signal processing)</span>"&gt;</span>quantization<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> followed by the use of prefix codes; these are often called "Huffman codes" even though most applications use pre-defined variable-length codes rather than codes designed using Huffman's algorithm.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1312"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="1313"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h2&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span
